 the offensive coach offers a boost of 8% to your attack ratings and a penalty of 11% to the defence ratings.

► the defensive coach offers a boost of 14% to your defence ratings and a penalty of 8% to your attack ratings.

► the neutral coach doesn't have a specific influence on your attack/defence ratings.*

*This calculations are made considering the neutral coach as a reference.


► The sports psychologists increase your team confidence and - directly - your attack ratings. It's good to have a minimum of 5 of them, to keep your confidence up, but this depends of how you can manage with the 30 staff members limit.

► The Passing skill of your inner midfielders offers a boost to your attack ratings (especially if they are played offensive and they've got a nice skill on Passing).


► If a player has played in two different positions during the week, the position that grants him the best training effect will be chosen at the update.


► When you play 1 Forward only, a good option is to maximize the attack on that side, playing the Forward Towards Wing or an Inner Midfielder Towards Wing (or even an Offensive/Normal WingBack).

► When you play PIC your Team Spirit will get a boost (multiply your actual TS with 1.33). When you play MOTS your TS will fall down with 50%.

► Your chances to score are distributed as they follow: 35% in the middle, 25% on each side (R/L) and 15% free kicks (direct and indirect FK).

► No matter if the HTs tried to lower the importance of the midfield rating, this is still the most important thing that can lead your team to victory. So do your best to possess your opponent (I'm not talking to the CA managers here :D).

Having Multi Skilled players with Playmaking skill will help you to have a better midfield rating (Defenders with PM, Wingers with PM, Defensive Forwards with PM).


► When you train Set Pieces, your Goalkeeper and your Set Pieces Taker will get a 25% bonus on training.

► When you sell a player it's not only your TS who may suffer a fall (depending on your player's character), but also your formation experience, if he was a regular player in your first 11.

► A good help to win a match is the Team Spirit. Having a high TS it's helpful to your midfield rating. The most possession you have, the most chances to score you'll get. A coach with a high leadership will help you to avoid losing too quick the TS.

► Try to be unpredictable, which will make it harder for your opponent to 'read' your tactics. Be diversified, don't play always the same tactic. 'Hide' your real final ratings with different substitutions and orders during the match (the final ratings are an average), especially when you're comfortable in the lead, but be cautious with that.

► In case of need, especially if you have a coach with low LS, you could surprise your opponent changing the coach just before the match starts (less time for your opponent to react, but pay attention on time), improving your team ratings where needed (defensive, neutral, offensive). A Solid coach/Poor LS costs 268.700 €. If you can afford it and you think it's worth, go for it.

► A coach with SOLID LEADERSHIP will drop his LS to Passable:
- in 112-150 days if he's low Solid LS
- in 150-224 days if he's medium Solid LS
- in 224-385 days if he's high Solid LS

► The formation experience (4-4-2, 3-5-2 etc) can drop only after a match, not after every HT update (or when you sell a player which used to be a regular one in your team).

► Trading tips: (8613)

► The overconfidence message in the beginning of the match never appears when you play MOTS! It may sound silly to play MOTS just to avoid that, but some could lose their 1st place in the League in the end of the season, PICing a match who may look easier than it is.
Be careful doing that if you'll have to play a Qualification match after this.

► When you get an overconfidence message in the beginning of the match, only your midfield is affected.

► If we consider a player playing at 100% of his capacity in Excellent form, then he will perform:
FORM	PERFORMANCE
Excellent	100%
Solid	96.70%
Passable	89.70%
Inadequate	82%
Weak	73.20%
Poor	62.90%
Wretched	50%
Disastrous	30.50%


► When you get a negative experience message in the match report all your ratings are affected and your team will perform as going into disorganisation, depending of both teams' experience. In the match report doesn't appear the level of disorganisation, but you can see that in midfield, as you'll notice the difference in possession, comparing to the first half (the final ratings are the average of all 90 minutes or possible extra ones).

► When you get a disorganization message in the match report, depending of the level your organisation drops, your team will perform as it follows:

ORGANISATION	PERFORMANCE
Solid	95-98%
Passable	89-94%
Inadequate	83-88%
Weak	76-82%
Poor	66-75%
Wretched	X-65%


► When you play against a Walkover team, you will win 5-0, get the formation experience and training for the full 90 min and the TS will be affected as usual (PIC, Normal, MOTS).

► There is an opinion (do not confuse it with a rule) that says that the match engine will consider first the general probability of winning for both teams, after that it will consider the exact score and in the end it will decide the distribution of the chances (which one will be goal and which one not).

This would explain somehow how at times a wretched attack rating will score against an utopian defending rating or how a divine attack rating doesn't score against a solid defending rating, for example.

► The total passing skill of all your outfield players determines your Attack On Wings / Attack In The Middle tactical skill.

► On the new engine there is no chance in the 45th and the 90th minute. The most chances seem to happen between min. 25-37.

► The efficiency of a coach - comparing to 100% of a Solid one - is:

COACH	EFFICIENCY
Excellent	105.30%
Solid	100%
Passable	90.90%
Inadequate	83.30%
Weak	76.90%
Poor	71.40%


► The Powerful and Quick players will never suffer a weather penalty event in the first half, if weather is Sunny.

► If you want to know more about the Team Spirit drop or PIC effect, you may want to consider this table: (http://img585.imageshack.us/img585/3466/teams...t.jpg) (at times that website is down).

► Having a high number of Head players your team will be more likely to score from the Head SE, but also to defend against your opponent's Headers. The influence of your Headers in scoring is A LOT BIGGER than in defending against your opponent's ones (corners). (13700898.133).

► Talking HatStats/LoddarStats, the "weakest" player in HT is the CDO, comparing to what is he losing and what is he bringing in the total team ratings. Don't get fooled about that, at times a CDO is all you may need to win a match, if you want just some extra midfield.

► After the match engine is analysing the possession, giving you an ordinary chance, it will compare the attack/defence ratings and if it's the case it will offer you the goal.
The scorer will be picked randomly (the FWs are more likely to be found on the scoring sheet).

► You can set up the Set Pieces Taker - in case your regular one is being substituted - using the Penalty Takers tab. If your SP Taker will be substituted, the second player from the Penalty Takers tab will do the job, not the substitute.

► If you need to improve your Team Spirit you can lower the training intensity. You could check exactly how much will that be here: (http://www.databased.at/hattrick/x-ray/?start...files) (Tools -> Matches -> TS vs TI). Be careful, you'll have to do that the latest Thursday morning and when you'll be back on 100% intensity you'll suffer a long term bad effect on your players' forms and your TS will drop badly.

► The harder you train, the better the squad's form becomes in general, and effects from training increase (make the connection with the previous trick).

► At the beginning of the season, after the TS reset, your team TS is composed medium (4.50).

► When your team gets a Special Event, it depends of the side where the match engine will give it to you (I'm talking about Technical vs Head, Quick for Wingers etc).

► When you buy a player, there is a chance that your TS may drop, depending of the player's character:
- Popular/Sympathetic - 0% chances for a TS fall
- Pleasant - 30%
- Controversial - 47%
- Nasty - 69%

► When you sell a player the chances for a TS drop are:
- Popular - 27% chances for a TS fall
- Sympathetic - 22%
- Pleasant - 12%
- Controversial/Nasty - 0%

► If a team has become ownerless it turns into a bot-team on the first of the three following points in time:
- before the 1st round of the Cup.
- after the 7th round of the league.
- after the 14th round of the league.

It takes 7 weeks of continuously NOT logging in to become 'a team without an owner'.

► You can make good money when you buy players, not only when you sell them. Buy cheap, especially in the end of the season, when prices are low!



► Do you need to know when and where the late international friendlies are played or if a player from TL got already the training/health update? Check all the updates in the HT-World: (http://www.tulospalvelu.biz/calendar/index.php) and (http://www.angelfire.com/theforce2/helghallen...e.htm).

► The experience of the player has an impact on a penalty competition only and NOT on a regular penalty kick (or set pieces chance) in the match.

Zorbas Supporter Diamond
Saint Lucifer
Grecja II.2
► The new ME may generate 15 ordinary chances in a match:
- 5 exclusive chances for team A. If team A's midfield rating is higher than the opponent's one, the probability of team A to be allocated such a chance increases. If such a chance won't be allocated, the chance will be lost.
- 5 exclusive chances for team B. If team B's midfield rating is lower than the opponent's one, the probability of team B to lose that chance increases. However, team A won't get that chance instead.
- 5 open chances - the team with a higher midfield rating has a bigger probability to be allocated such a chance. If one team is not allocated one of these chances, the opponent will get it instead.
Not all the chances are necessarily mentioned in the match report.

Apart of these 15 ordinary chances, in a match there are other extraordinary chances to score (SEs). Free kicks and penalties are counted as ordinary chances. Corner kicks are counted as special events.

Example: (253467325) - 18 chances (15 ordinary ones and 3 SEs).

(13541241.16), (13546116.91), (13541241.25), (13541241.202), (13541241.513), (13541241.207).

► Long Shots tactic level = 1.66*SC + 0.55*SP - 7.6
SC = outfield players average scoring
SP = outfield players average set pieces

Penalty on LS:
- Midfield: -5%
- Attack: -2,7%

(13160), (13124), (13125)

LS level - TOTAL
2 wretched - 15 to 18.4
3 poor - 18.5 to 20.3
4 weak - 20.4 to 23.0
5 inadequate - 23.1 to 24.6
6 passable - 24.7 to 25.9
7 solid - 26 to 27.8
8 excellent - 27.9 to 29.4
9 formidable - 29.5 to 31.1
10 outstanding - 31.2 to 33.1
11 brilliant - 33.2 to 34.2
12 magnificent - 34.3 to 36.2
13 worldclass - 36.3 to 37.8
14 supernatural - 37.9 to 40.0
15 titanic - 40.1 to 42.1
16 extraterrestial - 42.2 to 43.9
17 mythical - 44 to 45.5
18 magical - 45.6 to ?
19 utopian - 47.7
20 divine - ?

TOTAL = 3*avg(SC)+avg(SP)
where avg(SC) = average Scoring of all your ten field players
and avg(SP) = average Set Pieces of all your ten field players


► Team confidence comparison table, according to the number of psychologists: (http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/834/conf....png/).

► The weekly skill drop formula (for high skill): [(Skill-14,85)^2]/1000. If the player is more than 28 years old, an extra loss is added.

► When you buy a new player, matches played for other teams do not count for training purposes, although form and stamina updates do take account of these matches (for stamina training the player has to be healthy or maximum +1 injured). - (14422189.9).

► For DFKs only SP skill and XP are taken into account for the SP Taker. For IFKs, the ME takes into account the SP skill, XP, form and stamina. - (13923177.850)

► IFK:

def IFK = 0.4*mDef + .3*mSP + 0.1*SPgk + 0.08*GKgk

mAtt: outfield players attack skill average
mDEf: outfield players defence skill average

► the Goalkeeper contributes with:
- 86.6% of his GK skill to the Central Defence rating
- 42.5% of his Defending skill to the Central Defence rating
- 59.7% of his GK skill to the Side Defence ratings
- 27.6% of his Defending skill to the Side Defence ratings.

► The Central Defender Normal (CD) uses:
- 100% of his Defending skill for Central Defence
- 51.6% of his Defending skill for Side Defence
- 23.6% of his Playmaking skill for Midfield

►The Central Defender Offensive (CDO) is using:
- 31.8% of his PM skill for the Midfield rating
- 72.5% of his Defending skill for the Central Defence rating
- 37.8% of his Defending skill for the Side Defence rating

► The Central Defender Towards Wing (CDTW) is using:
- 16.5% of his PM skill for the Midfield rating
- 77.8% of his Defending skill for the Central Defence rating
- 71.1% of his Defending skill for the Side Defence rating
- 24.6% of his Winger skill for the Side Attack rating

► The Wing Back Defensive (WBD) will use:
- 6.6% of his Playmaking skill for your midfield rating
- 47.9% of his Defending skill for Central Defence rating
- 100% of his Defending skill for the Side defence rating
- 32.3% of his Winger skill for the Side Attack rating

► The Wingback Normal (WBN) uses:
- 45% of his Defending skill for Central Defence
- 91.9% of his Defending skill for Side Defence
- 16.7% of his Playmaking for Midfield
- 50.6% of his Winger skill for Side Attack

► The Wing Back Offensive (WBO) will use:
- 38.2% of his Defending skill for Central Defence
- 69.8% of his Defending skill for Side Defence
- 23% of his Playmaking skill for Midfield
- 61.8% of his Winger skill for Side Attack

► The Wingback Towards Middle (WBTM) uses:
- 68.3% of his Defending skill for the Central Defence
- 68.7% of his Defending skill for Side Defence
- 16.7% of his Playmaking skill for Midfield
- 27.9% of his Winger skill for Side Attack



---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

- 38.1% of his PM for midfield
- 8.5% of his Defending for Central Defence
- 18.0% of his Defending for Side Defence
- 13.5% of his Passing for Central Attack
- 24.6% of his Passing for Side Attack
- 100% of his Winger for Side Attack

► The Winger Towards Middle (WTM) uses:
- 57.4% of his PM for Midfield
- 56.4% of his Winger for Side Attack

- 24.4% of his Defending for Central Defence

- 21.5% of his Passing skill for Side Attack
- 12.4% of his Winger skill for Side Attack

► For Technical Defensive Forward (TDF) the contributions are the same with the DF, with the difference that his Passing skill contributes to the Side Attack with 27.9% instead of 21.5% (as it is for the non-technical defensive forward).

#2: Zorbas Supporter Diamond » #1: WszyscyWróć na górę! 23.08.2011 16:25

Zorbas Supporter Diamond
Saint Lucifer
Grecja II.2
1. INTRODUCTION

Weather: Sunny, Partially cloudy, Overcast, Rain.
Forecast for tomorrow: higher chances for same weather for tomorrow, smaller chances for a different weather.
The weather has an influence on the crowd for a match and also for some players' performance.

The extreme weather (Sunny and Rain) happen less often than Partially cloudy and Overcast (1/6).

Weather	Number	Percent
Rain	1300	14,8%
Cloudy	2952	33,7%
Partially cloudy	3079	35,1%
Sunny	1434	16,4%
Total	8765	100,0%

The study was made on almost 9.000 matches (hattrickinfo).

Prior to the changes in season 35 this is the effect the weather would have on crowd turnout:
- Sunny 100%
- Overcast 95%
- Cloudy 87%
- Rain 71%

Meaning that when the sky was cloudy there would be a crowd turnout of 87% compared to the turnout if the weather had been sunny. (hattrickinfo)

2. PLAYERS: SKILLS

Abbreviations: (http://hattrick-romania.ro/abrevieri-uzuale.html)

► Weekly skill drop formula: [(Skill-14,85)^2]/1000 (regardless the age; for the 28yo+ players an extra age drop will occur).
(http://acandio.blogspot.com/2011/01/hattrick-....html)


How good is your player?
The Hattrick Organizer (HO) program is the most accurate CHPP tool when it comes about the figures in the game (don't forget that HT is some kind of a chess game with dice though :D), helping you to find out the best tactics, the best individual orders, the best players etc.
Details: (15317757.1).

Latest full release: (http://sourceforge.net/projects/ho1/)
Latest beta: (http://ho1.sourceforge.net/development/)

► Talking HatStats/LoddarStats, the "weakest" player in HT is the CDO, comparing to what is he losing and what is he bringing in the total team ratings. Don't get fooled about that, at times a CDO is all you may need to win a match, if you want just some extra midfield.


► The Passing skill of your inner midfielders offers a boost to your attack ratings (especially if they are played offensive and they've got a nice skill on Passing).

► The average loss of performance when a player is bruised - (14695202.755):

3. PLAYERS: OTHER ATTRIBUTES

Experience

► The influence of player's XP:

Experience	Contribution
Non-existent	0%
Disastrous	5%
Wretched	8.80%
Poor	11.30%
Weak	13.40%
Inadequate	15.20%
Passable	16.80%
Solid	18.20%
Excellent	19.60%
Formidable	20.90%
Outstanding	22.10%
Brilliant	23.20%
Magnificent	24.30%
WorldClass	25.30%
Supernatural	26.30%
Titanic	27.30%
Extra-Terrestrial	28.20%
Mythical	29.10%
Magical	30.00%
Utopian	30.8%
Divine	31.60%


Formula: XP influence: =1+0,0716*ROOT(XP-1)

► XP points (1 XP level = 28 XP points):
Match type	XP points
National friendly match	0.1
International friendly match	0.2
League match	1
Cup match	2
U20/NT friendly match	2
Qualifying match	2
Hattrick Masters match	5
U20/NT official match	10
U20/NT World Cup (semi)final	20


► The experience of the player has a bigger impact on a penalty competition only than on a regular penalty kick (or set pieces chance) in the match.

► XP tool: (http://www.goanoei.nl/goht/goexp/)

Total Skill Index (TSI)
TSI is a measurement of how skilled a player is. TSI increases with training and can also increase (and decrease) with form. Don't pick a player for a position on the pitch taking into account exclusively his TSI or stars, but his useful skills.

Form
► If we consider a player playing at 100% of his capacity in Excellent form, then he will perform:
FORM	PERFORMANCE
Excellent	100%
Solid	96.70%
Passable	89.70%
Inadequate	82%
Weak	73.20%
Poor	62.90%
Wretched	50%
Disastrous	30.50%


► Form factor (from HO!) = ((form-0.5)/7)^0.45

Specialities
The Regainer speciality helps a player to recover quicker from an injury.

► The Powerful and Quick players will never suffer a weather penalty event in the first half, if weather is Sunny.

► Stamina factor (from HO!) = ((stamina+6.5)/14)^0.6
Stamina tools: (http://lizardopoli.altervista.org/staminia/)
(http://hagonline.org/uploads/tools/conditiepe...age=2)
(http://iht.smdesign.es/node/79)
(http://img854.imageshack.us/i/contributiontab....png/)
(http://hattrick-romania.ro/procente-rezistenta....).

#5: Zorbas Supporter Diamond » #1: WszyscyWróć na górę! 23.08.2011 16:27

Zorbas Supporter Diamond
Saint Lucifer
Grecja II.2
► Injuries
Maximum injury: +4 weeks (it could be 4.80 for example, though).

The bruised players' performance is affected by injury and a second possible injury's period is added on top of that one they already have by bandage.

► Loyalty: (http://croack.altervista.org/it/prima-squadra...delta).

If you buy a previous YA player you do not regain the motherclub loyalty.
If you transferlist a player (by mistake or not), but you'll buy him back at the end of those 3 days he's on the TL, he won't lose his loyalty, as he didn't actually leave the team.

4. LINEUP: THE BASICS
Starting line-up and substitutes



POSITIONS (legend)

► the Goalkeeper contributes with:
- 86.6% of his GK skill to the Central Defence rating
- 42.5% of his Defending skill to the Central Defence rating
- 59.7% of his GK skill to the Side Defence ratings
- 27.6% of his Defending skill to the Side Defence ratings.



---------------------------------------------------------------------------------



► The Central Defender Normal (CD) uses:
- 100% of his Defending skill for Central Defence
- 51.6% of his Defending skill for Side Defence
- 23.6% of his Playmaking skill for Midfield

►The Central Defender Offensive (CDO) is using:
- 31.8% of his PM skill for the Midfield rating
- 72.5% of his Defending skill for the Central Defence rating
- 37.8% of his Defending skill for the Side Defence rating

► The Central Defender Towards Wing (CDTW) is using:
- 16.5% of his PM skill for the Midfield rating
- 77.8% of his Defending skill for the Central Defence rating
- 71.1% of his Defending skill for the Side Defence rating
- 24.6% of his Winger skill for the Side Attack rating

► The Wing Back Defensive (WBD) will use:
- 6.6% of his Playmaking skill for your midfield rating
- 47.9% of his Defending skill for Central Defence rating
- 100% of his Defending skill for the Side defence rating
- 32.3% of his Winger skill for the Side Attack rating

► The Wingback Normal (WBN) uses:
- 45% of his Defending skill for Central Defence
- 91.9% of his Defending skill for Side Defence
- 16.7% of his Playmaking for Midfield
- 50.6% of his Winger skill for Side Attack

► The Wing Back Offensive (WBO) will use:
- 38.2% of his Defending skill for Central Defence
- 69.8% of his Defending skill for Side Defence
- 23% of his Playmaking skill for Midfield
- 61.8% of his Winger skill for Side Attack

► The Wingback Towards Middle (WBTM) uses:
- 68.3% of his Defending skill for the Central Defence
- 68.7% of his Defending skill for Side Defence
- 16.7% of his Playmaking skill for Midfield
- 27.9% of his Winger skill for Side Attack

5. MATCH: THE BASICS

The basics of the match simulation
The moment when an event happens is picked randomly. At that specific time, the match engine analisis the possession (the midfield ratings of both teams) and decides if or which team gets a chance to score. The Attack rating of the team who got the chance "fights" the Defence rating of the opponent team on that side (for example the Right Attack rating will "fight" the opponent's Left Defence rating). If the Attack rating is higher than the opponent's Defence rating on that side, the chance to score a goal is higher. The scorer will be picked randomly, but the players with a higher Scoring skill are more likely to be found on the scoresheet.

Chances

► Your regular chances to score are distributed as they follow: 35% in the middle, 25% on each side (R/L) and 15% free kicks (direct and indirect FK).

► The new ME may generate 15 ordinary chances in a match:
- 5 exclusive chances for team A. If team A's midfield rating is higher than the opponent's one, the probability of team A to be allocated such a chance increases. If such a chance won't be allocated, the chance will be lost.
- 5 exclusive chances for team B. If team B's midfield rating is lower than the opponent's one, the probability of team B to lose that chance increases. However, team A won't get that chance instead.
- 5 open chances - the team with a higher midfield rating has a bigger probability to be allocated such a chance. If one team is not allocated one of these chances, the opponent will get it instead.
Not all the chances are necessarily mentioned in the match report.

Apart of these 15 ordinary chances, in a match there are other extraordinary chances to score (SEs). Free kicks and penalties are counted as ordinary chances. Corner kicks are counted as special events.

Example: (253467325) - 18 chances (15 ordinary ones and 3 SEs).

(13541241.16), (13546116.91), (13541241.25), (13541241.202), (13541241.513), (13541241.207).

Zorbas Supporter Diamond

Grecja II.2
Team rating is the rating you should focus on

Think team ratings, not player ratings. Use the Foxtrick add-on to notice different statistics in the team ratings after the match ends (HatStats, probabilities etc) - (http://www.ht-foxtrick.com/forum/portal.php).

► When you play 1 Forward only, a good option is to maximize the attack on that side, playing the Forward Towards Wing or an Inner Midfielder Towards Wing (or even an Offensive/Normal WingBack).

► No matter if the HTs tried to lower the importance of the midfield rating, this is still the most important thing that can lead your team to victory. So do your best to possess your opponent (I'm not talking to the CA managers here :D).

Having Multi Skilled players with Playmaking skill will help you to have a better midfield rating (Defenders with PM, Wingers with PM, Defensive Forwards with PM).

► A good help to win a match is the Team Spirit. Having a high TS it's helpful to your midfield rating. The most possession you have, the most chances to score you'll get. A coach with a high leadership will help you to avoid losing too quick the TS.

Grecja II.2
► Try to be unpredictable, which will make it harder for your opponent to 'read' your tactics. Be diversified, don't play always the same tactic. 'Hide' your real final ratings with different substitutions and orders during the match (the final ratings are an average), especially when you're comfortable in the lead, but be cautious with that.


► On the new engine there is no chance in the 45th and the 90th minute. The most chances seem to happen between min. 25-37.

► There is an opinion (do not confuse it with a rule) that says that the match engine will consider first the general probability of winning for both teams, after that it will consider the exact score and in the end it will decide the distribution of the chances (which one will be goal and which one not).

This would explain somehow how at times a wretched attack rating will score against an utopian defending rating or how a divine attack rating doesn't score against a solid defending rating, for example.

6. TRAINING

The training takes place taking into account:
- what training type you have set up on the training update
- the coach and the assistants
- how many minutes a player has played in the League/Cup/friendly match in a week
- if the player has played on a trainable position during the week.

In the manual table you'll find:
- without brackets - maximum effect on training - 100%
- single brackets - smaller effects - 50%
- double brackets - very small effects - osmosis training - 16%.

Training intensity
ST = TI - (TI*SS%)

ST = specific training received
TI = training intensity
SS% = stamina share

► If a player has played in two different positions during the week, the position that grants him the best training effect will be chosen at the update.

► When you train Set Pieces, your Goalkeeper and your Set Pieces Taker will get a 25% bonus on training.

► The harder you train, the better the squad's form becomes in general, and effects from training increase.

► When you buy a new player, matches played for other teams do not count for training purposes, although form and stamina updates do take account of these matches (for stamina training the player has to be healthy or maximum +1 injured and they get 50% stamina of the new team).

Training predictor: (http://www.htspain.es/index.php?pag=train_calc)
(http://hattrick-romania.ro/predictor-antrenam....html)

Goalkeeper training tool: (http://www.hottrick.org/hattrick_keeper_tool.php)

(http://www.htdaytrading.com/index.php)
(http://www.pharmacist.dk/Barthon/) - the wages suffered changes though
(http://pauliasi4ht.wordpress.com/)

7. THE COACH

► The efficiency of a coach - comparing to 100% of a Solid one - is:

COACH	EFFICIENCY
Excellent	105.30%
Solid	100%
Passable	90.90%
Inadequate	83.30%
Weak	76.90%
Poor	71.40%



Leadership:
► A coach with SOLID LEADERSHIP will drop his LS to Passable:
- in 112-150 days if he's low Solid LS
- in 150-224 days if he's medium Solid LS
- in 224-385 days if he's high Solid LS

Coach type:
► the offensive coach offers a boost of 8% to your attack ratings and a penalty of 11% to the defence ratings.

► the defensive coach offers a boost of 14% to your defence ratings and a penalty of 8% to your attack ratings.

► the neutral coach doesn't have a specific influence on your attack/defence ratings.*

*This calculations are made considering the neutral coach as a reference.

Francja VI.520
1. INTRODUCTION

Weather: Sunny, Partially cloudy, Overcast, Rain.

Forecast for tomorrow: since May 2024 (/Help/SystemStatus/Archive/Default.aspx?Messa...6&p=1), the weather for the day after is no more a forecast that may or may not change, but it shows the actual weather with total certainty. This helps users set the lineup one day prior to the match knowing 100% sure what the weather will be.

The weather has an influence on the crowd for a match and also for some players' performance (depending on their specialty).

The extreme weather (Sunny and Rain) happen less often than Partially cloudy and Overcast (1/6).

Full data set (904 211 random samples):



Rain	Overcast	Partially
cloudy	Sunny	Total
143 937	311 419	310 098	138 757	904 211
15.919%	34.441%	34.295%	15.345%	100%

Prior to the changes in season 35 this is the effect the weather would have on crowd turnout:
- Sunny 100%
- Overcast 95%
- Cloudy 87%
- Rain 71%

Meaning that when the sky was cloudy there would be a crowd turnout of 87% compared to the turnout if the weather had been sunny. (hattrickinfo)

2. PLAYERS: SKILLS

► Note that since December 2016 (/World/News/Archive.aspx?messageId=57073&isEd...als=0), there is no longer any skill drops due to high skills (above titanic), there is only be skill drops due to age. Instead, this same skill drop effect from higher skills was be turned into slower training speed for those same skills, making the net effect very similar to before that reform.

► Since December 2024 (/World/News/Archive.aspx?messageId=9487&isEdi...als=0), the skill drops of Monday have been merged with the end of week's training update.


► How good is your player?

The Hattrick Organizer (HO) program is the most accurate CHPP tool when it comes about the figures in the game (don't forget that HT is some kind of a chess game with dice though :D), helping you to find out the best tactics, the best individual orders, the best players etc.
Details: (17079553.1).

last stable version: (https://github.com/akasolace/HO/releases/tag/st...)

User Guide for HO: (https://github.com/akasolace/HO/wiki)


► TSI (Total Skill Index)

TSI is a measurement of how skilled a player is. TSI increases with training and can also increase (and decrease) with form. Don't pick a player for a position on the pitch taking into account exclusively his TSI or stars, but his useful skills.

TSI = (1.03*Def^3 + 1.03*PM^3 + 1.03*Sc^3 + 1.0*Ps^3 + 0.84*Wg^3)^2 * St^0.5 * Fm^0.5 / 1000

TSIgk = 3 * Gk^3.359 * Fm^0.5

(With Solid=6) (Note: non-existent stands for 0, disastrous starts at 0,01 and goes to 1. And so on, making solid 6,01-7,00, and not like generally accepted from 7 to 7,99)
- TSI Calculator: (https://hattrick.chechesa.com/en)


► HTMS
The HTMS is the training potential of a player, regarding his skills and his age.
- The current HTMS of a player is based on his current skills, and is calculated using this formula:
HTMS = f(Gk) + f(Def) + f(PM) + f(Wg) + f(Ps) + f(Sc) + f(SP).

You have to cumulated the HTMS given for each skill in the table of this post (17024376.56)

- The HTMS-28 or the HTMS potential at 28 y.o. gives an idea of "how good" the player will be at 28 years-old. You have to cumulate the current HTMS calculated before, with the values depending on his age in the following post: (17024376.57)
- See also (17568840.43) and [post=https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1_igKkTBGuy96Uavyv36yopeDkBCc7-dDnFHENzF4kU4/edit#gid=103550019]

- Tools to calculate current HTMS / HTMS potential of a player: (https://www.fantamondi.it/HTMS/index.php?page...ng=en)
(https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1ZVIdh...18153)
If you're using foxtrick: you'll have a module called HTMSPoints that will show two values in the player page: the current points and the points at 28 years in the format: xxx (yyy)


► Talking HatStats/LoddarStats, the "weakest" player in HT is the CDO, comparing to what is he losing and what is he bringing in the total team ratings. Don't get fooled about that, at times a CDO is all you may need to win a match, if you want just some extra midfield.

► The Passing skill of your inner midfielders offers a boost to your attack ratings (especially if they are played offensive and they've got a nice skill on Passing).

► About Set Pieces training limitation in regard to 25% bonus for GK/nominated player, there is a limit of 1.0 level of increase (17354587.795)

3. PLAYERS: OTHER ATTRIBUTES

Experience

► Formulas from WesselV1 (11234483): (17371940.86): XP is not applied directly to the skills, but to the ratings, following the approximated formulas below:
- Side defence and midfield: 0.36 * (1 – 0.85 ^ (exp level))
- Central defence and side attack: 0.36 * 7 / 8 * (1 – 0.85 ^ (exp level))
- Central attack: 0.36 * 4 / 5 * (1 – 0.85 ^ (exp level))

Complement from Tasos here (17445499.339): there is no a direct influence with the way you define it on the sectors, such as attack_right + experience, but the experience affects the contribution each player has to the sector.

► The influence of player's XP in each skill (previous version, before WesselV1' studies):

Disastrous	+0

Formula: XP influence: = log (experience) * 4/3

You can calculate the total skill as affected by experience (based on the formula above, before WesselV1' studies) with the Tool created by Murzim (8649722), using the player`s XP table above: (http://www.evdaimon.com/hattrick/xp_skill2.php).

► XP points: 1 XP level = 100 XP points
See table of the official manual here: (/Help/Rules/PlayerAttributes.aspx)

► The experience of the player has a bigger impact on a penalty competition only than on a regular penalty kick (or set pieces chance) in the match.

► The amount of experience a certain player gets is minute based, just as training. A player can not gain more than 90 minutes of experience from each match.

► If a player doesn't play a full minute (e.g. he gets red-carded as soon as he enters the field), he will not receive any training (neither skill, nor form, nor XP).

Detailed table of loyalty bonus vs number of days in your club (from Danfisico (3232936)): (15305653.2)

If you buy a previous YA player you do not regain the motherclub loyalty.
If you transfer-list a player (by mistake or not), but you'll buy him back at the end of those 3 days he's on the TL, he won't lose his loyalty, as he didn't actually leave the team.

Form

► The better form a player is in, the better he will perform. If we consider a player playing at 100% of his capacity in Excellent form, then he will perform (influence on each skill):

FORM	PERFORMANCE
Excellent	100%
Solid	96.70%
Passable	89.70%
Inadequate	82%
Weak	73.20%
Poor	62.90%
Wretched	50%
Disastrous	30.50%

► Form factor (from HO!) = ((form-0.5)/7)^0.45

Theoretical average form according to hired specialists:
(http://ht.alergromania.ro/tools/average-playe...ator/)

► On the player page you can see a player's "current form", which is the figure applied for matches, but there's a hidden "background form", which is used to compute where the player's form is heading. For more details, read the chapter about form in the official manual: (/Help/Rules/PlayerAttributes.aspx)

► To improve the background form of your players, make them play once a week, with a high training intensity, hire a form coach, and have a coach and assistent coaches with high levels for both.


Specialities: See (17517965.29) for more details.


Tools
Tool of giupino82 (10376800) to calculate the real skills of a player with all his attributes (form, experience, etc...), and compare them to the skills of another player: (https://hattrickradar.netsons.org/radar.php)

performance = % of health.
player is bruised, health = [0.9; 1.0)
average health - 0.95

► Since January 2017, the duration of the injury depends on the age of the player and the level of your staff medic. Injuries are no longer general, they happen to a specific part of the body. Be careful when fielding a bruised player! If he gets injured again, it is much more likely that the new injury happens in the same spot as the previous one, and if it does, this new injury will be slightly more serious than it would otherwise have been.

► Healing of a player stops at the 41st birthday.

► (17445499.8) from HT-Tasos: There isn't any difference in the injury length depending on the type of injury (card or random).

► Since Editorial of September 4th, 2024 (/World/News/Archive.aspx?messageId=9315&isEdi...als=0):
- A shift has been made from long-term injuries to short-term ones, reducing the likelihood of severe, prolonged injuries
- The risk of getting additional players injured has decreased for every injury you get during a match, in order to have fewer matches where one team gets many injuries.
- There is though now a minor risk of injury during training, but only for healthy players who participated in a match. At most, only one player can be injured during training, and such injuries are never more serious than a bruise.


► Fouls and cards
(14695202.22) Agreeability, Aggressiveness & Honesty vs. Fouls, Cheating & Cards
(14695202.26) Aggressiveness / Honesty vs. Cards (Yellow / yellow+red / red)
(14695202.29) Aggressiveness + Honesty combo vs. Card (after foul)
(14695202.31) Aggressiveness + Honesty combo vs. Card (after cheating)
(14695202.51) Rates of injury (25% injury rate) for yellow card that is a foul
(17572304.263) Rates of injury extended to an entire team composed of players based on aggressiveness

Relative Contribution Values

NB: [Relative Values] are only describing what e.g. player A's playmaking skill would contribute to the midfield, if e.g. played in the central defense compared to if he was played as an inner midfielder:
X absolute value / Y absolute value = relative value


As you can see; Relative Values are purely found from Absolute Values.
See also example here: (17517965.662)
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

► the Goalkeeper (GK) contributes with:
- 87% of his GK skill to the Central Defence rating
- 61% of his GK skill to the Side Defence ratings
- 35% of his Defending skill to the Central Defence rating
- 25% of his Defending skill to the Side Defence ratings.


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------


► The Central Defender Normal (CD) uses:
- 100% of his Defending skill for Central Defence
- 26% of his Defending skill for Side Defence
- 25% of his Playmaking skill for Midfield

► The Right Central Defender Normal (RCD) uses:
- 100% of his Defending skill for Central Defence
- 52% of his Defending skill for Right Side Defence
- 0% of his Defending skill for Left Side Defence
- 25% of his Playmaking skill for Midfield

► The Left Central Defender Normal (LCD) uses:
- 100% of his Defending skill for Central Defence
- 0% of his Defending skill for Right Side Defence
- 52% of his Defending skill for Left Side Defence
- 25% of his Playmaking skill for Midfield

►The Central Defender Offensive (CDO) is using:
- 73% of his Defending skill for the Central Defence rating
- 20% of his Defending skill for the Side Defence rating (20% for each side)
- 40% of his PM skill for the Midfield rating

► The Central Defender Towards Wing (CDTW) is using:
- 67% of his Defending skill for the Central Defence rating
- 81% of his Defending skill for the Side Defence rating
- 26% of his Winger skill for the Side Attack rating
- 15% of his PM skill for the Midfield rating

► The Wing Back Defensive (WBD) will use:
- 43% of his Defending skill for Central Defence rating
- 100% of his Defending skill for the Side defence rating
- 10% of his Playmaking skill for your midfield rating
- 45% of his Winger skill for the Side Attack rating

► The Wingback Normal (WBN) uses:
- 38% of his Defending skill for Central Defence
- 92% of his Defending skill for Side Defence
- 15% of his Playmaking for Midfield
- 59% of his Winger skill for Side Attack

► The Wing Back Offensive (WBO) will use:
- 35% of his Defending skill for Central Defence
- 74% of his Defending skill for Side Defence
- 20% of his Playmaking skill for Midfield
- 69% of his Winger skill for Side Attack

► The Wingback Towards Middle (WBTM) uses:
- 70% of his Defending skill for the Central Defence
- 75% of his Defending skill for Side Defence
- 20% of his Playmaking skill for Midfield
- 35% of his Winger skill for Side Attack

► The Forward Normal (FW) uses:
- 100% of his Scoring skill for Central Attack

- 66% of his Scoring skill for Central Attack

- 53% of his Passing skill for Central Attack
- 31% of his Passing skill for Side Attack
- 13% of his Winger skill for Side Attack

► For Technical Defensive Forward (TDF) the contributions are the same as the Defensive Forward (DF), with the difference that his Passing skill contributes to the Side Attack with 41% instead of 31% (as it is for the non-technical Defensive Forwards).

► There are some agglomeration penalties, in case you play 2 or 3 players on the same central position. Those penalties occur to all the skills of the players from that specific central compartment of your team and they are:

- 2 Central Defenders: -3.6%
- 3 Central Defenders: -10%

- 2 Inner Midfielders: -6.5%
- 3 Inner Midfielders: -17.5%

- 2 Forwads: -5.5%
- 3 Forwards: -13.5%


Absolute Contribution Values

► This link is a completely contribution table based on Hattrick Organizer's player contributions (absolute values):
(https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1zYuBi...aring)

► The simplest way to describe a player contribution is to only focus on skills multiplied with the absolute value for that specific position, for that specific skill.

Eg. we have a player with the following skills:

Goalkeeper: Disastrous (1)
Defense: Solid (7)
Playmaking: Excellent (8)
Winger: Excellent (8)
Passing: Inadequate (5)
Scoring: Passable (6)

Placing him as a Right Central Defender Normal (RCD) in a standard 4-4-2 lineup, means there are 2 central defenders. Then, you should look up the absolute values in the table linked before.

His contribution will be:

● Left defense: DE (7) × 0,00 = 0
● Right defense: DE (7) × 0,503 = 3,521 (Disastrous High)
● Central defense: DE (7) × 0,602 = 4,214 (Disastrous Very High)

● Midfield: PM (8) × 0,113 = 0,904 (Disastrous Very Low (despite being lower than 1, everything between 0,001 and 1,999 equals to Disastrous Very Low)

● Left attack: 0
● Right attack: 0
● Central attack: 0

Link to the HatStat table: (https://wiki.hattrick.org/index.php?title=HatStats)

► Man Marking:

- Editorial: (/World/News/Archive.aspx?messageId=7578&isEdi...als=0)
- Devblog: (https://devblog.hattrick.org/2017/12/let-the-...egin/)

To sum up :
- Man Marking counts as an individual order : it can be used only if your man-marker plays normal (confirmed by Tasos here (17147468.39) and here (17147468.73))

- You can do only one man-marking by game. The Man-Marker should be within the 11 players starting the game, or can be set as a substitute (his man-marking will be active as soon as he entered the field).

- Man Marking affects Defending, Playmaking, Winger, Passing and Scoring for the man-marker, and Playmaking, Winger, Passing and Scoring for the man-marked player. Then, whatever is affected by those skills is like a chain (e.g. tactic levels, probability to get a SE).
Set Pieces and Goalkeeping are not affected.

- If the man-marked player is on the “opposite” sector, then your man-marking player will lose 50% of his contribution. By "opposite" sector, we mean:
- Any central defender vs Any forward
- Any wingback vs Any winger (even if the winger is not on the same side than the wingback)
- Any midfielder vs Any midfielder
- In any other case, your player will suffer of 65% loss of his performance.
- If there is a change of position during the match, man-marking effect will be recalculated



Table for theoretical penalties
for the man-marking player

Man-marker | Man-marked player	FW	W	IM
CD	-50%	-65%	-65%
WB	-65%	-50%	-65%
IM	-65%	-65%	-50%


- If the opponent’s player you want to man-mark is not on the field, then your man-marking player will lose 10% of his contribution.

- Formula used to calculate the Man Marking effect:
penalty = defending ^ 3.5 / (defending ^ 3.5 + highest_skill ^ 3.5)


With:
- defending = defending skill of the man-marker
- highest skill = highest skill of the man-marked player (Set Pieces excluded)
All the skills are modified first by form, stamina, XP, loyalty, mother club bonus & health (and weather events if there are).

- Bonus for the man-marking player on his Defending skill (important: this bonus is considered only for the man-marking calculation, not for the whole game):
- +10% for Powerful players
- +5% for non-spec players

- Bonus / penalties for the man-marked player vs. specialities, applied on his highest skill:
- -8% for Technical players
- +8% for Unpredictable players

So it is:
- for Unpredictable players:
penalty = defending ^ 3.5 / (defending ^ 3.5 + 1.08*highest_skill ^ 3.5)
- for Technical players:
penalty = defending ^ 3.5 / (defending ^ 3.5 + 0.92*highest_skill ^ 3.5)

- Calculator created by shadow___ (10488141) about the penalty on the man-marked player: (https://neverlastinger.github.io/ManMarkingCa...ator/)

Important: the skills to use in this calculator are not the real skills, but the skills after considering the bonus & penalties due to form, stamina, loyalty, MC bonus, XP & health (and weather events if there are).
You can use this tool from giupino82 (10488141) to calculate the skills updated with all the attributes:
(http://hattrickradar.netsons.org/radar.php)
Note that this last tool doesn't take into account the bonus / malus of 5% for weather effects (which should be considered before calculating the penalty of man-marking with shadow___ 's tool).

5. MATCH: THE BASICS

The basics of the match simulation

The moment when an event happens is picked randomly. At that specific time, the match engine analisis the possession (the midfield ratings of both teams) and decides if or which team gets a chance to score. The Attack rating of the team who got the chance "fights" the Defence rating of the opponent team on that side (for example the Right Attack rating will "fight" the opponent's Left Defence rating). If the Attack rating is higher than the opponent's Defence rating on that side, the chance to score a goal is higher. The scorer will be picked randomly, but the players with a higher Scoring skill are more likely to be found on the scoresheet.

Chance to score: (14695202.231)

Chances

► Your regular chances to score are distributed as they follow: 35% in the middle, 25% on each side (R/L) and 15% free kicks (direct and indirect FK).

Stats from nickarana confirming these numbers (thanks to Live data of around 100k matches)(17493341.5)

► The new ME may generate 15 cycles that may include a total of 15 ordinary chances in a match:
- 5 exclusive chances for team A. If team A's midfield rating is higher than the opponent's one, the probability of team A to be allocated such a chance increases. If such a chance won't be allocated, the chance will be lost.
- 5 exclusive chances for team B. If team B's midfield rating is lower than the opponent's one, the probability of team B to lose that chance increases. However, team A won't get that chance instead.
- 5 open chances - the team with a higher midfield rating has a bigger probability to be allocated such a chance. If one team is not allocated one of these chances, the opponent will get it instead.
Not all the chances are necessarily mentioned in the match report.

► Apart of these 15 ordinary chances, in a match there are other extraordinary chances to score (SEs). Free kicks and penalties are counted as ordinary chances. Corner kicks are counted as special events.

There can be many events in 1 cycle. Each cycle is based on 6 phases in the following order:

a) Special Event;
b) Chance;
c) Potential Counter Attack, if the Chance was played but wasn't scored;
d) Yellow/Red Card;
e) Injury;
f) Team Confusion.


In (18016).

And all of them can happen in one cycle (except, if chance scored).

Example: (253467325) - 18 chances (15 ordinary ones and 3 SEs).

(13541241.16), (13546116.91), (13541241.25), (13541241.202), (13541241.513), (13541241.207).

► Possession VS Chances you should get (in average): (https://devblog.hattrick.org/2016/02/and-on-t...tion/)

► Probability to get chance for lower midfield team, where a = lower midfield rating and b = higher midfield rating:
- According to Tasos' Devblog (https://devblog.hattrick.org/2016/02/and-on-t...tion/): a^2/2b^2
- According to real probabilities from the match report: a^3/(a^3+b^3)
Based on nickarana's studies here: (17572304.373), the 2nd formula is correct.

Note: you can use midfield ratings or ball possession values, it is the same as the formula is based on a ratio.

► Formula for real probabilities - attack (a) vs defense (d):
0,92 * a^3,5 / (a^3,5 + d^3,5)
Verification of formula: (https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1ImjY6...aring)
Real ratings (from CHPP) should be used, taking into account a -0.75 gap (so if attack=12 and defense = 13.5 for example in the match report, the values to use in the formula should be a = 11.25 and d = 12.75).

(https://wiki.hattrick.org/index.php?title=Glo...edule)
(https://wiki.hattrick.org/index.php?title=Friendly)
(https://fcclogo.kaoztribe.net/Countries.php)

Note:
Some times were updated on April 26th, 2024 (/World/News/Archive.aspx?messageId=77671&isEd...als=0), and might not be reflected yet in some of the previous links.


Home team advantage

► The influence on midfield rating:


Coefficient type	value
Playing Normal&Away	100%
Playing CA	93%
Playing at home	119.892%
Playing derby(away team)	111.493% •
Playing PIC	83.945%
Playing MOTS	111.49%

• away team only, the home team gets the 119.892%, as usual.
Coefficients are multiplied, for example:
- playing home & MOTS 119.892%*111.49%=133.67%
- playing home & PIC & CA : 119,892 % * 83.945 % * 93 % = 93,598%

Possession formula: Possession % = Midfield1 / (Midfield1 + Midfield2) *100%

Team rating is the rating you should focus on

Think team ratings, not player ratings. Use the Foxtrick add-on to notice different statistics in the team ratings after the match ends (HatStats, probabilities etc) - (https://foxtrick-ng.github.io/).

► When you play 1 Forward only, a good option is to maximize the attack on that side, playing the Forward Towards Wing or an Inner Midfielder Towards Wing (or even an Offensive/Normal WingBack).

► No matter if the HTs tried to lower the importance of the midfield rating, this is still the most important thing that can lead your team to victory. So do your best to possess your opponent (I'm not talking to the CA managers here :D).

► Having Multi Skilled players with Playmaking skill will help you to have a better midfield rating (Defenders with PM, Wingers with PM, Forwards with PM).

► A good help to win a match is the Team Spirit. Having a high TS is helpful to your midfield rating. The most possession you have, the most chances to score you'll get. A coach with a high leadership will help you to avoid losing too quick the TS.

► Try to be unpredictable, which will make it harder for your opponent to 'read' your tactics. Be diversified, don't play always the same tactic. 'Hide' your real final ratings with different substitutions and orders during the match (the final ratings are an average), especially when you're comfortable in the lead, but be cautious with that.

► On the new engine, there can be chances at 90+0, 90+1 and 90+2 (and 90+3...), as extra time has been added in the ME. Be aware that the compensation time label is a Foxtrick feature and sometimes the minute of an event is not correct. Eg. this game had a goal at minute 90 + 2, although match report label shows minute 90 +7: (614995797).

► The new HT-Live takes a 5 minutes pause before extra time starts.

► Use your Tactic Assistant wisely: it enables you to diversify the style of your game and balance your ratings more offensively/defensively :
- If you have a defensive or an offensive coach, you can go up to a neutral style of play with a tactical assistant level 5.
- If you have a neutral coach, you can reach a style of play between 50% defensive and 50% offensive with a tactical assistant level 5.

► When you play against a Walkover team, you will win 5-0, get the formation experience and training for the full 90 min and the TS will be affected as usual (PIC, Normal, MOTS). There is no gain of Experience for your players, though.
Note that since April 5th, 2023, the possibility of walkovers has been reduced: (/World/News/Archive.aspx?messageId=75189&isEd...als=0):
When a manager fails to field a valid formation, other club functionaries will step in and do it in their place. As long as the club has enough players in the squad, walkovers should no longer happen.
It is always better for the team to be led by their human manager. Any intervention by functionaries in this way will lead to lower team spirit, form, confidence and formation experience, albeit only during this match. The tactical bonus of the coach will also be ignored. Training will happen as usual.

6. TRAINING

The training takes place taking into account:
- what training type you have set up on the training update
- the coach and the assistants
- how many minutes a player has played in the League/Cup/friendly match in a week
- if the player has played on a trainable position during the week.

In the manual table you'll find:
- without brackets - maximum effect on training - 100%
- single brackets - smaller effects - 50%
- double brackets - very small effects - osmosis training - 16%.

Training intensity

ST = TI - (TI*SS%)

ST = specific training received
TI = training intensity
SS% = stamina share

► If a player has played in more than one position during the week, and more than 90 minutes in total, the minutes and positions that grant him the best training effect, will be chosen at the update, while obeying the maximum of 90 minutes per week.

► When you train Set Pieces, your Goalkeeper and your Set Pieces Taker will get a 25% bonus on training.

► The harder you train, the better the squad's form becomes in general, and effects from training increase.

► When you buy a new player, matches played for other teams do not count for training purposes, stamina is counted like he had played 0 minutes (equal to 50% stamina training), although form update does take account of these matches.

► If you reduce your Training intensity, your TS (Team Spirit) will increase. Although, this is not recommendable due to the negative form effects it might cause on your squad the weeks after this trick is used.
If you want to use the TS trick, you must decrease the training intensity before the last update which precede the training update (e.g. if the training update is on Friday morning, the TI must be decrease before Thursday morning).

Training intensity trick calculator:

http://www.ht-tools.eu/trainingintensity (dead link)
(https://ht.8ic.ro/trainingintensity)
Note that the TS management (via the TS-trick) can also be seen on the new training page of Hattrick.

HT-Tools: http://www.ht-tools.eu/training (dead link) (might be offline for a while according to HT-Tasos explanation here: (17135358.3))
